\"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain is implemented across multiple files in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository, primarily in the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver directory. The architecture consists of several key layers:\\n\\n## Core Admission Chain\\n\\nThe foundational admission chain mechanism is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go, which implements `chainAdmissionHandler` - a slice of admission handlers that sequentially processes admission requests. The chain calls either `Admit()` for mutation or `Validate()` for validation on each handler that handles the given operation.\\n\\nAdmission handler types are defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go, which specifies the `Interface`, `MutationInterface`, and `ValidationInterface` that webhook plugins must implement.\\n\\n## Webhook Plugin Infrastructure\\n\\nThe webhook plugins are built on a generic foundation:\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go** - The `Webhook` base class that provides common webhook infrastructure including configuration management, initialization, and dispatch orchestration.\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go** - Defines the `Dispatcher` interface that webhook-specific implementations must satisfy, and the `Source` interface for retrieving webhook configurations.\\n\\n## Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nMutating and validating webhooks implement separate dispatchers:\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go** - The `mutatingDispatcher` implements the `Dispatcher` interface and handles calling mutating webhooks. It manages webhook invocation ordering, re-invocation logic when webhooks mutate the object, and handles JSON patch responses by applying patches to the request object.\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go** - The `validatingDispatcher` handles validating webhooks. Unlike mutating webhooks, validating webhooks are called in parallel for performance optimization and cannot mutate the request object.\\n\\n## Webhook Plugins\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go** - Implements the `Plugin` struct for mutating webhooks with an `Admit()` method that delegates to the generic webhook dispatcher.\\n\\n- **staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go** -
